[30;1m44 | [0m[35minformation from two or more records that are believed to belong to the same[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35mentity. Record linkage is used to link data from multiple data sources or to[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35mfind duplicates in a single data source. In computer science, record linkage[0m
[30;1m47 | [0m[35mis also known as data matching or deduplication (in case of search duplicate[0m
[30;1m48 | [0m[35mrecords within a single file).[0m
